				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							years = 5
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8133.8.1 = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					k_iron_isles = {
						holder_scope = { has_nickname = nick_the_red_kraken }
					}
				}
				k_westerlands = {

					}

		}

	}
	8129.4.1 = { #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.1.1 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
				}
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.1 = {	#Hightower host enforced his submission

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.10.22 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = supporting_king

					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}

				}

					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT

							years = 5

							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100

	name = "Алан"	# a lord, grandson of Lyman Beesbury, Married Lynett Hightower
	dynasty = 282

	religion = "the_seven"
	culture = "wineman"

	father = 3010282 # Osbert Beesbury
	mother = 3007287

	8092.1.1 = { birth = yes }
	8108.1.1 = { add_trait = knight add_trait = trained_warrior }
	8109.1.1 = { add_spouse = 5010285 } # Lynett Hightower
	8129.4.1 = { #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = against_king
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
			}
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = {
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			c_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					ROOT = {
						join_attacker_wars = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.4 = {
		death = {
			death_reason = death_execution # Died in captivity in the Dance of Dragons.
		}
	}
}

		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.1.1 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
				}
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.1 = {	#Hightower host enforced his submission
		add_trait = knight
		add_trait = skilled_warrior
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.10.22 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = supporting_king
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							years = 5
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

3016278 = {
	name = "Гюнтор"	# a lord
	dynasty = 278

	religion = "the_seven"
	culture = "reachman"

	father = 3009278

	8083.1.1 = { birth = yes }
	8099.1.1 = { add_trait = knight add_trait = trained_warrior }
	8129.4.1 = { #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.1.1 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
				}
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { year = 8197 } }
							ROOT = {
								join_attacker_wars = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.1 = {	#Hightower host enforced his submission
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.10.22 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = supporting_king
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = {
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							years = 5
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8142.1.1 = { death = yes }
